# D&D Beyond full image catalog for Forgotten Realms config research

Generated from the full D&D Beyond posts archive pass for Forgotten Realms/location art research. This file intentionally includes non-location images, repeated UI assets, covers, monsters, NPCs, maps, and encounter art because the review pass needs the whole visual pool.

The crawler scanned numeric posts listing pages 1-57. Pages 58 and 59 repeated page 57, so page 57 was the archive end at the time of the pass. From 1,533 listing entries, the Forgotten Realms/location keyword filter selected 164 candidate posts/resources. 152 candidate pages were fetched, 144 of them yielded images, and 676 image occurrences collapsed to 491 distinct image URLs below.

Categorization is machine-assisted. Use the source links, headings, alt text, and area hints to promote good candidates back into `location-art-resources.md` or later into config review.

## Category Counts

| Category | Unique images |
|----------|---------------|
| Locations, Areas, And Scenery | 37 |
| Maps And Route References | 26 |
| Monsters And Creatures | 119 |
| NPCs, Characters, Factions, And Player Options | 77 |
| Items, Props, And Handouts | 19 |
| Books, Products, And Promo Art | 40 |
| DDB UI, Tools, And Repeated Avatars | 24 |
| Generic Adventure Scenes And Encounter Art | 72 |
| Uncategorized Or Needs Review | 77 |

## Notes

- Duplicate image URLs are shown once, with occurrence counts and representative source links.
- `Area hints` are inferred from the image URL, section heading, artist/context line, and alt text; source-title-only hints are shown separately as `Source context hints` when useful.
- Some thumbnail URLs are the exact URLs used by older D&D Beyond posts. They are still D&D Beyond-hosted attachment URLs, but may not be the highest resolution asset available.
- The catalog keeps product and UI images because they were extracted from relevant candidate pages; they should not be used as runtime location art without a deliberate review.

### 185. A cleric holds a glowing magical artifact in her hands.
